## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0019 [0x32] ExtData[1]->MainSpeed = 40* * 0.1
  1: 0x001C [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: EventEntity moves to X=168.855*, Z=-200.937*, Y=20.100*
  2: 0x0024 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: Update entity position (mode=1)
  3: 0x0026 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
